            <div style="TEXT-ALIGN: right"><font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Item
1</font></div>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">
          <div>&#160;</div>
          <div align="center">
            <table bgcolor="white" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%">
                <tr>
                  <td width="50%"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;<img src="abn_header.jpg" alt=""></font></td>
                  <td valign="top" width="50%"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;<img src="rbs-logo.jpg" alt=""></font></td>

          <div>&#160;</div>

        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">
          <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #000000">Amsterdam</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #000000">, </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #000000">8 February 2010</font></font></div>
          <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
          <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">ABN
AMRO completes legal demerger</font></div>
          <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 49.15pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">&#8220;I am delighted to announce that we
have reached a significant milestone in the separation process. This has led us
a step closer to the creation of two independent banks, the ABN AMRO Bank and
The Royal Bank of Scotland NV. This would not have been achieved without the
tremendous contribution of people from both organisations<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#8221;&#160;&#160;&#160;
</font></font></font></div>
          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 49.15pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Gerrit
Zalm</font></div>
          <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">On 6 February 2010,
the businesses of ABN&#160;AMRO acquired by the Dutch State were legally
demerged from the RBS acquired businesses. As a result, there are now two
separate banks within ABN&#160;AMRO Holding N.V., The Royal Bank of Scotland
N.V. (&#8216;RBS N.V.&#8217;) and the new entity named ABN&#160;AMRO Bank N.V., each
licensed separately by the Dutch Central Bank. Both banks will be governed by
the current managing and supervisory boards of ABN&#160;AMRO Holding N.V. until
the legal separation of the new ABN AMRO Bank N.V. from ABN AMRO Holding
N.V.</font></div>
          <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The legal
separation involves the transfer of the new ABN&#160;AMRO Bank N.V. to a holding
company that has been established by the Dutch State. This transfer is expected
to take place within two months of the legal demerger and is subject to approval
by the Dutch Central Bank. The new ABN AMRO Bank N.V. will then become an
independent bank with new managing and supervisory boards, operating under Dutch
Central Bank supervision and unrelated to the RBS Group.</font></div>
          <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The legal demerger
and the global renaming to The Royal Bank of Scotland N.V. are significant
milestones for the integration of the businesses and assets acquired by RBS. At
legal separation, new managing and supervisory boards will be appointed for RBS
N.V., which will operate under Dutch Central Bank supervision.</font></div>
          <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
          <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Appendix
1</font></div>
          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">ABN AMRO completes
legal demerger of Dutch State acquired businesses and associated legal
renaming</font></div>
          <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Appendix
2</font></div>
          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">September 2009 Pro
Forma Financial Information</font></div>
          <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">For
more information, please contact:</font></div>
          <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>

      <div style="TEXT-ALIGN: right"><font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Item
2</font></div>
      <div>&#160;</div>
    </div>
    <div style="TEXT-ALIGN: right"><font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold">APPENDIX
1</font></div>
    <div>&#160;</div>
    <div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">ABN
AMRO completes legal demerger of Dutch State acquired businesses and associated
legal renaming</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div>
        <table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%">
            <tr bgcolor="#f3f3f3">
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="74%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; COLOR: #808080; FONT-FAMILY: arial"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">Certain
      definitions</font></font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">Throughout this press release,
      '</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #808080">ABN</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #808080"> AMRO
      H</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #808080">olding</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">' means </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">ABN</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080"> AMRO Holding N.V.&#160;&#160;The
      term '</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #808080">ABN</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #808080">
      AMRO</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">'
      refer</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">s</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080"> to </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">ABN</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080"> AMRO </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">Holding and its consolidated
      subsidiaries.&#160;&#160;'</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #808080">RBS
      N.V.</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">' and 'the
      </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #808080">Demerging
      Company</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">' means The
      Royal Bank of Scotland N.V. (previously named </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">ABN</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080"> AMRO Bank N.V.) and its
      consolidated subsidiaries.&#160;&#160;The '</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #808080">Acquiring
      Company</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">' means
      </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">the new entity named
      </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">ABN</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080"> AMRO Bank N.V. (previously named
      </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">ABN</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080"> AMRO II N.V.). '</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #808080">EUR</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">' refers to euros, while
      '</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #808080">USD</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">' refers to US
      dollars.</font></font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">The terms '</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #808080">Consortium</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">' and '</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #808080">Consortium
      Members</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">' refer to The
      Royal Bank of Scotland Group plc (</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #808080">RBS</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #808080">
      Group</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">), Fortis N.V.,
      Fortis SA/NV (</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #808080">Fortis</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">) and Banco Santander S.A.
      (</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #808080">Santander</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">) </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">that</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080"> jointly acquired </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">ABN</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080"> AMRO Holding N.V. on </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">17 October 2007</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080"> through </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">RFS</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080"> Holdings B.V.&#160;&#160;On 3
      October 2008 the State of the Netherlands (</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #808080">Dutch
      State</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">) acquired
      Fortis Bank Nederland (Holding) N.V., including the interest in
      </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">RFS</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080"> Holdings B.V.</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080"> that represents the acquired
      activities of </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">ABN</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080"> AMRO</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">,</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080"> and effectively became the
      successor of Fortis in the Consortium Shareholder
      Agreement.</font></font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">Furthermore, all references to
      </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">ABN</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080"> AMRO Bank N.V. (where it is clear
      from the context that such reference is not a reference to the Acquiring
      Company) shall be deemed to be a reference to The Royal Bank of Scotland
      N.V.</font></font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">The term '</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #808080">l</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #808080">egal
      </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #808080">d</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #808080">emerger</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">' refers to the legal demerger
      (</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080; FONT-STYLE: italic">juridische
      splitsing</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">)
      </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">under</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080"> Title 2:7 of the Dutch Civil Code
      of </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">ABN</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080"> AMRO</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080"> into the Acquiring Company and
      the Demerging Company</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">, pursuant to the legal demerger.
      T</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">he </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">Dutch</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">State</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080"> acquired businesses </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">were transferred </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">to the Acquiring Company from the
      Demerging Company </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">on</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">6 February 2010</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">. </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">C</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">ertain subsidiaries and assets and
      liabilities were separately transferred to the Acquiring Company
      </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">prior to</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080"> the execution of the legal
      demerger and some further assets and liabilities </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">will</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">be </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #808080">separately transferred to the
      Acquiring Company around the same time or shortly after the execution of
      the legal demerger.</font></font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>
        </table>
      </div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">On
6 February 2010 ABN AMRO successfully executed the deed of demerger in
accordance with the demerger proposal filed with the Amsterdam Chamber of
Commerce on 30 September 2009, thereby demerging the majority of the Dutch State
acquired businesses.&#160;&#160;Additionally, as part of the overall separation
process, some subsidiaries and assets and liabilities were separately
transferred to the new legal entity ahead of the execution of the legal
demerger. Furthermore, some further assets and liabilities will be separately
transferred to the Acquiring Company around the same time or shortly after the
execution of the legal demerger.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Effective at the
same date, the existing legal entity ABN AMRO Bank N.V., from which the Dutch
State acquired businesses were demerged, was renamed The Royal Bank of Scotland
N.V.&#160;&#160;The legal entity into which the Dutch State acquired businesses
were demerged was also renamed, from ABN AMRO II N.V. to ABN AMRO Bank
N.V.&#160;&#160;Both the Demerging Company and the Acquiring Company will remain
wholly owned by ABN AMRO Holding until the latter is legally separated from ABN
AMRO Holding.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The demerger
proposals (excluding the description of assets and liabilities) and pro forma
financial information as of 31 December 2008 and 30 June 2009 reflecting the
impact of the legal transfers and demergers on ABN AMRO are available at <font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #0000ff; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">www.abnamro.com</font>.&#160;&#160;The
complete demerger filing, including a description of assets and liabilities to
be transferred, was filed with the Amsterdam Chamber of Commerce on 30 September
2009.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">This represents the
successful execution of the first step in a two step process ABN AMRO chose to
effect the legal separation of the assets and liabilities acquired by the Dutch
State.&#160;&#160;The second step, "legal separation", will result in the
transfer of the shares of the Acquiring Company from ABN AMRO Holding to a new
holding company fully owned by the Dutch State and independent of ABN AMRO
Holding. After the legal separation, ABN AMRO Holding will be renamed RBS
Holdings N.V.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>
      <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
        <div id="FTR">
          <div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left">
          </div>
        </div>
        <div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
          <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">1</font></div>
          <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
            <hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
          </div>
        </div>
        <div id="HDR">
          <div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right">
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">ABN AMRO Holding
was acquired by a consortium of banks through RFS Holdings B.V. on 17 October
2007.&#160;&#160;The consortium consisted of RBS (38%), Fortis (34%) and
Santander (28%).&#160;&#160;On 24 December 2008 the Fortis Bank Nederland
(Holding) N.V. stake in RFS Holdings B.V. was transferred to the Dutch State,
following the acquisition by the Dutch State in October 2008 of Fortis Bank
Nederland (Holding) N.V., including its stake in RFS Holdings B.V.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Until legal
separation, ABN AMRO will continue to be governed by ABN AMRO Holding&#8217;s managing
and supervisory boards and regulated on a consolidated basis with capital
adequacy, liquidity measures and exposures being reported to and regulated by
the Dutch Central Bank.&#160;&#160;ABN AMRO's capital ratios continue to exceed
the minimum tier 1 and total capital ratios of 9% and 12.5% respectively (as set
under Basel I by the Dutch Central Bank <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">(De Nederlandsche Bank)</font>
during the separation period of ABN AMRO) and are adequate to cover for stress
scenarios.&#160;&#160;ABN AMRO continues to comfortably exceed the regulatory
liquidity requirements.&#160;&#160;ABN AMRO and its shareholder have taken steps
to ensure that at legal separation each individual, separating bank will be
adequately capitalised and has a sound liquidity position.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">RBS N.V. will be an
integral part of the RBS Group and will principally contain international
lending, international transaction services and equities businesses of the RBS
Group.&#160; These remaining activities will continue to be subject to Dutch
Central Bank supervision and on a consolidated basis as part of the RBS Group be
subject to UK Financial Services Authority supervision.&#160; Due to the change
in the operating model of RBS N.V. compared to pre-acquisition ABN AMRO Bank
N.V., a licence renewal was granted by the Dutch Central Bank on 3 February
2010.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The majority of the
businesses acquired by the Dutch State, consisting of the Dutch commercial and
retail banking, Dutch and international private clients and diamond businesses,
were transferred to the Acquiring Company at or shortly before the legal
demerger.&#160;&#160;However, during the period between the legal demerger and
legal separation a small &#8216;tail&#8217; of predominantly international businesses will
continue to be transferred to the Acquiring Company.&#160;&#160;The exact timing
of these transfers will be determined by, amongst other things, the granting of
regulatory approvals in the countries in which the businesses operate. The
Acquiring Company was granted a banking licence on 13 January 2010.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Following the legal
demerger and until legal separation, the managing and supervisory boards of RBS
N.V. and of the Acquiring Company will be the same as the managing and
supervisory boards of ABN AMRO Holding.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Banking
license</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">On
13 January 2010 the Dutch Central Bank granted a banking license to the
Acquiring Company for engaging in universal banking business in the
Netherlands.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">On
3 February 2010 the Dutch Central Bank granted a continuation of its existing
banking license to RBS N.V.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Capital
ratios</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The following table
shows the pro forma capital ratios as at 30 September 2009 on the basis of the
Basel I capital accord for both ABN AMRO Holding and the Acquiring Company, both
after the effect of the legal demerger and including the effect of capital
actions executed on 23 December 2009 and the planned capital distribution as
described below.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>

      </div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Capital
actions new ABN AMRO Bank N.V.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The capital actions
of the Dutch State for the benefit of the Dutch State acquired businesses to be
transferred to the Acquiring Company, executed on 23 December 2009, consisted of
the issue of two Mandatory Convertible Securities. The first of these was issued
by the Demerging Company in the amount of EUR 967 million and has been demerged
together with the assets and liabilities of the Dutch State acquired businesses
in accordance with the legal demerger filing dated 30 September 2009 to the
Acquiring Company. The second of these was in the amount of EUR 833 million and
was issued directly by the Acquiring Company to cover expected losses in respect
of the EU Remedy business disposal as described below. The latter issuance did
not contribute to the capital ratios as of 31&#160;December 2009, since a
banking license was granted to the Acquiring Company in 2010.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">As
a consequence of the capital actions described above, the capital position of
the Acquiring Company will exceed the current regulatory minima as set by the
Dutch Central Bank for ABN AMRO (Tier I capital ratio 9%, Total capital ratio
12.5%) under the agreed Basel I transitional regime during the period of
separation of ABN AMRO.&#160;&#160;These capital actions are also aimed to
adequately satisfy the Dutch Central Bank regulatory requirements in accordance
with Basel II.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Capital
actions RBS N.V.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The capital actions
completed by the RBS Group for the benefit of the future RBS N.V. consisted of
the inclusion of assets in the UK&#8217;s Asset Protection Scheme through a guarantee
agreement between The Royal Bank of Scotland plc and RBS N.V., and an equity
capital contribution of EUR 3.6 billion.&#160;&#160;As a result, the RBS
acquired businesses are more than adequately capitalised under the current Basel
I transitional regime and are aimed to be adequately capitalised at a level
commensurate with the requirements of the future RBS N.V., post legal
separation, under Basel&#160;II.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Capital
distribution</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The completion of
the capital actions described facilitated the execution of the legal demerger
and supports the future legal separation of the Acquiring Company from ABN AMRO
Holding planned to be completed approximately two months after the legal
demerger.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The boards of ABN
AMRO Holding have approved and have obtained necessary approval from the Dutch
Central Bank for the distribution of EUR 7.5 billion of capital to the parent of
ABN AMRO Holding, RFS Holdings B.V., for the benefit of Santander. This
distribution was effected on 5 February 2010. The boards of ABN AMRO Holding
have furthermore resolved to make a further distribution for an amount in the
range of EUR&#160;1.2 to 1.5 billion for the benefit of Santander, subject to
Dutch Central Bank approval, immediately before legal separation. After such
further distribution, the indirect interest of Santander in ABN AMRO will have
decreased to its share in the remaining Shared Assets.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>

      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Ratings</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The
Acquiring Company</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">On
5 February 2010, Standard &amp; Poor&#8217;s announced that it assigned A+ (long term)
/ A-1 (short term) ratings with a negative outlook to the Acquiring Company upon
legal demerger.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">On
20 January 2010, Fitch Ratings announced that it expects to assign A+ (long
term) / F1+ (short term) ratings with a stable outlook to the Acquiring Company
upon legal demerger.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">On
21 January 2010, Moody&#8217;s Investors Service assigned provisional Aa3 (long term)
/ P-1 (short term) ratings with a negative outlook to the Acquiring Company upon
legal demerger. Moody&#8217;s Investors Services will assign final ratings upon legal
demerger.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The
Demerging Company</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">On
7 January 2010, Standard &amp; Poor&#8217;s announced that it expects to assign A+
(long term) / A-1 (short term) ratings with a stable outlook to the Demerging
Company upon legal demerger.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">On
5 February 2010, Fitch Ratings reaffirmed that it expects to assign AA- (long
term) / F1+ (short term) ratings with a stable outlook to the Demerging Company
upon legal demerger.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">On
5 February 2010, Moody&#8217;s Investors Service assigned provisional A2 (long term) /
P-1 (short term) ratings with a stable outlook to the Demerging Company upon
legal demerger.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Debt
allocation</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The allocation of
debt instruments to Consortium Members has been finalised as part of the legal
demerger process.&#160;&#160;The debt instrument allocation list is available at
<font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #0000ff; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">www.abnamro.com/investors/investors.cfm</font>.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">As
part of the finalisation, the USD 150 million 7.13% subordinated notes 2093
(previously reported in Central Items) have been allocated to the RBS acquired
businesses and will, therefore, continue as an obligation of RBS
N.V.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The USD 250 million
7.75% subordinated lower tier 2 notes 2023, while economically allocated to the
Dutch State acquired businesses, remain a legal obligation of RBS N.V. until
their intended transfer in the second quarter of 2010 to the new ABN AMRO Bank
N.V. These notes can not be transferred to the Acquiring Company as part of the
Dutch legal demerger process, because they are governed by US law.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Risk
Factors</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Set out below are
the risk factors pertaining to the legal demerger process.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Recourse
of investors due to legal demerger and cross liability</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Following the legal
demerger, ABN AMRO has demerged into two entities, being the Demerging Company
and the Acquiring Company with effect from 6 February 2010. After that date, in
principle investors will only have recourse to the entity to which the relevant
assets and liabilities have been transferred for payments in respect of the
appropriate securities.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">However, under
article 2:334t of the Dutch Civil Code, the Demerging Company, after legal
demerger, remains liable to the creditors for obligations which transferred from
the Demerging Company to the Acquiring Company in the event that the Acquiring
Company cannot meet its obligation to those creditors.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Similarly, after
legal demerger, the Acquiring Company is liable to the creditors for obligations
that remain in the Demerging Company, in the event that the Demerging Company
cannot meet its obligation to those creditors.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">In
each case, the liability of a party for the obligations of the other party and
vice versa relates only to obligations existing at the date of legal
demerger.&#160;&#160;The liability will cease to exist upon</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>
      <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
        <div id="FTR">
          <div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left">
          </div>
        </div>
        <div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
          <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">4</font></div>
          <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
            <hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
          </div>
        </div>
        <div id="HDR">
          <div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right">
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">expiration of the
obligations. Furthermore, the Demerging Company's liability for (in short)
monetary obligations is limited to the equity retained at legal demerger,
amounting to EUR 4.0 billion. The Acquiring Company's liability for (in short)
monetary obligations is limited to the amount of equity acquired at legal
demerger, which amounts to EUR 1.8 billion.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The Demerging
Company will put in place arrangements to mitigate the risks of its liability to
the creditors which transferred from the Demerging Company to the Acquiring
Company.&#160;&#160;The Acquiring Company will also put in place arrangements to
mitigate the risks of its liability to the creditors which remain with the
Demerging Company. Such arrangements include the provision of collateral upon
the occurrence of certain events, which will be put in place by legal
separation. Each of the Demerging Company and the Acquiring Company will hold
the regulatory capital agreed with the Dutch Central Bank for any residual
risks.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The
joint and several liability of ABN AMRO Holding for the debts of the Acquiring
Company will be revoked following the anticipated legal separation</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">ABN AMRO Holding
deposited two statements pursuant to Section 2:403 of the Netherlands Civil Code
with the Commercial Register of the Chamber of Commerce in Amsterdam (403
Declaration), each declaring that ABN AMRO Holding is jointly and severally
liable for the debts resulting from the legal acts of ABN AMRO Bank N.V., the
Demerging Company in its form prior to the legal demerger, and of the Acquiring
Company.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Following the legal
demerger, these 403 Declarations continue to be applicable. Upon the legal
separation, the 403 Declaration relating to the Acquiring Company, the demerged
and transferred subsidiaries and, partially, to the Demerging Company, will be
revoked, provided that all of the relevant conditions of Section 2:404 of the
Dutch Civil Code are met. Consequently the joint and several liability of ABN
AMRO Holding for the debts resulting from legal acts of the Acquiring Company
(including remaining liability for legal acts of the Acquiring Company which
arose prior to the date of revocation of the 403 Declaration), the demerged and
transferred subsidiaries and of the Demerging Company to the extent it relates
to the split-off to the Acquiring Company pursuant to the legal demerger, will
be terminated.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">ABN AMRO Holding
filed its intention to terminate any such remaining liability with the Amsterdam
Chamber of Commerce on 2 December 2009. By filing the intention to terminate the
remaining liability, a creditor objection period of two months was initiated,
which ended on 2&#160;February 2010.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">ABN
AMRO&#8217;s legal demerger and legal separation process creates additional risks for
ABN AMRO's business and stability</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">ABN AMRO is going
through a period of transition and change, which poses additional risks to ABN
AMRO&#8217;s business including (i) ABN AMRO&#8217;s ability to manage the break up of ABN
AMRO in a controlled manner while minimising the loss of business, (ii) ABN
AMRO's ability to retain key personnel during the transition and (iii) enhanced
operational and regulatory risks during this period. During this period of
transition and change and as a result of the legal demerger and upcoming legal
separation, the Demerging Company and the Acquiring Company will remain
interdependent with respect to certain business areas, for which they will <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">inter alia</font> provide
certain&#160;services&#160;to each other.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Integration
of the Acquiring Company with Fortis Bank (Nederland) N.V.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">On
21 November 2008, the Dutch State announced its intention to integrate the Dutch
State acquired businesses of ABN AMRO with Fortis Bank (Nederland) N.V. (&#8216;FBN&#8217;)
after completion of the legal demerger and legal separation process. The
integration of the Acquiring Company with FBN is subject to the completion of
the sale by the Acquiring Company to Deutsche Bank AG of NEW HBU II N.V. and IFN
Finance B.V.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The integration
process of the Acquiring Company with FBN could be delayed due to <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">inter alia</font> delays regarding
the structuring of the legal merger of the two entities or delays in approval or
additional terms and conditions of supervisory and regulatory
bodies.&#160;&#160;Failure or delay in this </font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>
      <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
        <div id="FTR">
          <div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left">
          </div>
        </div>
        <div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
          <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">5</font></div>
          <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
            <hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
          </div>
        </div>
        <div id="HDR">
          <div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right">
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">integration may
adversely affect the stand alone operation of the Acquiring Company and may
therefore adversely affect the Acquiring Company&#8217;s results and financial
condition.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Major
Shareholder and change of control</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">As
at the date of the legal demerger, ABN AMRO Holding is the sole shareholder of
the Acquiring Company.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">As
a consequence of and as from the legal separation, the shares of the Acquiring
Company will be transferred from ABN AMRO Holding to a new holding company fully
owned by the Dutch State, named ABN AMRO Group N.V., and independent of ABN AMRO
Holding, which will after separation be renamed RBS Holdings N.V.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The Dutch State has
announced its intention to integrate the Acquiring Company with FBN after
completion of the legal separation process.&#160;&#160;The Dutch State is not
involved in the day-to-day management of the Acquiring Company, and has
expressed the intention not to be involved in the day-to-day management of the
combined entity once the Acquiring Company has merged with FBN.&#160;&#160;The
Dutch State has stated its intention to privatise the combined bank not earlier
than 2011.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">EU
Remedy</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">ABN AMRO Bank N.V.
and Deutsche Bank AG signed the Share Purchase Agreement&#160;&#160;confirming
the agreements reached for the sale of NEW HBU II N.V. (NEW HBU II) and IFN
Finance B.V. (IFN Finance) on 23 December 2009.&#160;&#160;The sale price agreed
upon for NEW HBU II and IFN Finance, including a guarantee provided for 75% of
the credit losses ('credit umbrella') and an amount for other liabilities and
costs, is EUR 700 million.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">With the signing,
the sale is now closer to completion.&#160;&#160;The final steps in the process
prior to the closing thereof are the transfer of the NEW HBU II shares to the
Acquiring Company, the legal demerger of the majority of the businesses acquired
by the Dutch State into the Acquiring Company and the legal separation of the
Acquiring Company.&#160;&#160;The closing of the NEW HBU II and IFN Finance
transaction is expected to take place thereafter in the early spring of
2010.&#160;&#160;ABN AMRO<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">&#160;</font>has considered the
impact of the transaction on results and capital ratios and considers that the
transaction will have a negative impact of between EUR 800 and EUR 900 million
on results.&#160;&#160;The total loss on the transaction includes a provision
for the credit umbrella.&#160;&#160;The new ABN AMRO Bank N.V.<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">&#160;</font>expects to account for
these losses when, after legal separation, the conditions for effecting the
closing have been met.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Documents
available</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">On
8 February 2010, ABN AMRO Holding, the Demerging Company and the Acquiring
Company also published pro forma financial information as of 31 December 2008
and 30 September 2009 reflecting the financial impact of the legal transfers and
demergers on ABN AMRO (the <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">September 2009 Pro Forma Financial
Information</font>). This information includes an updated organisational chart
and is attached as Appendix 2.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Further information
on the separation of ABN AMRO is available at <font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #0000ff; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">www.abnamro.com</font>
and <font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #0000ff; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">www.rbs.com</font>.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The Dutch
Registration Document and copies of all documents incorporated by reference in
the Registration Document are accessible at <font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #0000ff; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">www.abnamro.com</font>
and at <font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #0000ff; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">http://markets.rbs.com/bparchive</font>
and can be obtained, on request, free of charge, by writing or telephoning, ABN
AMRO Press Office, Gustav Mahlerlaan 10, PO Box 283, 1000 EA Amsterdam, The
Netherlands, telephone (+31) 0(20) 628 8900, e-mail <font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #0000ff; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">pressrelations@nl.abnamro.com</font></font></div>

          <div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
            <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
            </div>
            <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
              <hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
            </div>
          </div>
          <div id="HDR">
            <div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right">
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Background</font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">At the date of
demerger, ABN AMRO Bank N.V. was renamed to The Royal Bank of Scotland N.V.
(hereinafter RBS N.V.) and ABN AMRO II N.V. was renamed ABN AMRO Bank
N.V.&#160;&#160;Until legal separation both RBS N.V. and ABN AMRO Bank N.V. will
be governed by the ABN AMRO Holding N.V. managing and supervisory boards and
regulated on a consolidated basis with capital ratios, liquidity measures and
exposures being reported to and regulated by the Dutch Central Bank. For an
overview of the liabilities issued by ABN AMRO Bank N.V. that have been
allocated to the Dutch State acquired businesses and a list of the liabilities
remaining as legal obligations of RBS N.V., refer to <font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #0000ff; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">www.abnamro.com</font>.</font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The Royal Bank of
Scotland Group plc (&#8216;RBS Group&#8217;) and the State of the Netherlands (&#8216;Dutch
State&#8217;) continue to work towards the legal separation of the Dutch State
acquired businesses from the residual RBS acquired businesses into two separate
viable banks, each with its own banking license and each adequately capitalised
at the time of legal separation. On 13 January 2010 the Dutch Central Bank
granted a banking license to ABN AMRO Bank N.V. for engaging in universal
banking business in the Netherlands. On 3 February 2010 the Dutch Central Bank
granted a continuation of its existing banking license to RBS N.V.</font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">After legal
separation, ABN AMRO Holding N.V. will be renamed RBS Holdings
N.V.&#160;&#160;RBS N.V. will remain a wholly owned subsidiary of RBS Holdings
N.V., which in turn will remain wholly owned by RFS Holdings B.V. RFS Holdings
B.V. will be substantially owned by the RBS Group after separation. RBS N.V.
principally contains international lending, international transaction services
and equities businesses of the RBS Group.</font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">ABN AMRO Bank N.V.
will become a wholly owned subsidiary of a newly incorporated entity ABN AMRO
Group N.V. which in turn will be wholly owned by the Dutch State.&#160;&#160;ABN
AMRO Bank N.V. serves Dutch commercial and retail banking clients, Dutch and
international private clients, and diamond businesses.</font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The diagram below
shows the demerger and separation process in steps.</font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">
          <div align="center"><img src="p3.jpg" alt=""></div>
        </div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
        <div>
          <table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%">
              <tr valign="top">
                <td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">1.</font></div>
                </td>
                <td>
                  <div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The Dutch
      State&#8217;s part of the assets and liabilities that are not yet allocated to
      any of the Consortium shareholders, the so-called <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">Shared Assets</font>, are not
      included in this overview.</font></div>
                </td>
              </tr>
          </table>
        </div>
        <div>
          <table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%">
              <tr valign="top">
                <td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">2.</font></div>
                </td>
                <td>
                  <div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The structure
      shown represents the position after a transitional phase, during which the
      Dutch State and Banco Santander S.A.&#160;&#160;will continue to hold a
      stake in RFS Holdings B.V. commensurate to their holding in remaining
      Shared Assets and any other businesses subject to later
      separation.</font></div>
                </td>
              </tr>
          </table>
        </div>

        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The purpose of this
document is to provide pro forma financial information to supplement the
demerger press release by ABN AMRO Holding N.V. with updated information about
the new legal structure of ABN AMRO.&#160;&#160;The legal demerger is a
significant event and therefore the update is required to provide investors with
relevant historical financial information on a pro forma basis allowing an
assessment of the impact of the demerger.&#160;&#160;The pro forma financial
information has been prepared for illustrative purposes only on the basis of
estimates and assumptions which are preliminary.&#160;&#160;The pro forma
information addresses a hypothetical situation and does not represent the actual
position or the results of either ABN AMRO Holding N.V. or ABN AMRO Bank
N.V.</font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The pro forma
financial information includes the following pro forma information for both ABN
AMRO Holding N.V. and ABN AMRO Bank N.V. (i) a pro forma Statement of Financial
Position as at 30 September 2009, (ii) a pro forma Income statement for the nine
months ended 30 September 2009, (iii) a pro forma Statement of Financial
Position as at 31 December 2008, (iv) a pro forma income statement for the year
ended 31 December 2008, and (v) Notes to the pro forma financial
information.&#160;&#160;This pro forma financial information should be read in
conjunction with the financial information and the related notes for the 9
months ended 30 September 2009 published in the press release of ABN AMRO
Holding N.V. on 25 November 2009 and the financial statements and the related
notes thereto for the year ended 31 December 2008.</font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The unaudited pro
forma financial information may be subject to change because management has not
finalised their detailed assessment of key estimates and judgements which is
part of the preparation process of the consolidated financial statements for the
year ended 31 December 2009. Management is not aware of any matters that could
impact ABN AMRO Holding N.V.&#8217;s results and financial position as presented in
the pro forma financial information. The audited consolidated financial
statements of ABN AMRO Holding N.V. for the year ended 31 December 2009 will be
available at the end of March 2010.</font></div>

                </td>
                <td align="left" valign="top" width="96%">
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">This column
      removes the effect of reclassification of balances between ABN AMRO
      Holding N.V. and ABN AMRO Bank N.V. that were intercompany transactions
      before the legal demerger. The reclassification is performed to show ABN
      AMRO Holding N.V. (to be renamed RBS Holdings N.V. and including RBS N.V.)
      as if it were a standalone legal entity.</font></div>
                </td>
              </tr>

                </td>

      pro forma financial information.</font></div>

financial information has been prepared on the following basis:</font></div>

                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: symbol, serif">&#183;</font></div>
                </td>
                <td valign="top" width="92%">
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">The pro forma
      condensed consolidated statement of financial position of ABN AMRO Holding
      N.V. at 30 September 2009 and 31 December 2008 is presented to show the
      effect of the legal demerger of ABN AMRO Bank N.V. and is based upon the
      respective consolidated balance sheets at 30 September 2009 and 31

                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: symbol, serif">&#183;</font></div>
                </td>
                <td valign="top" width="92%">
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">The pro forma
      condensed consolidated income statement of ABN AMRO Holding N.V. for the
      nine months ended 30 September 2009 and the year ended 31 December 2008 is
      presented to show the effect of the legal demerger of ABN AMRO Bank N.V.
      and is based upon the respective consolidated income statements for the
      nine months ended 30 September 2009 and the year ended 31 December 2008 of
      ABN AMRO Holding N.V. and ABN AMRO Bank N.V. as if the proposed
      transaction had occurred on 30 September 2009 and 31 December
      2008.</font></div>

N.V., after the demerger, continues to include assets and liabilities that have
not yet been settled between the consortium shareholders, the so-called &#8220;Shared
Assets&#8221;, in which each of the consortium shareholders has a joint and indirect
interest.&#160;&#160;The net value of the assets and liabilities that are
currently expected to remain for an interim period in ABN AMRO Holding N.V.
amounts to EUR 6.9 billion negative at 30 September 2009.&#160;&#160;As part of
the legal demerger, capital related to the demerged businesses transferred to
ABN AMRO Bank N.V. However sufficient capital remains in ABN AMRO Holding N.V.
to cover the Dutch State interest in the Shared Assets.</font></div>

        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">At the date of
legal demerger, EUR 4.2 billion of EUR 203.0 billion of assets and EUR 4.1
billion of EUR 196.1 billion liabilities, which are included the pro forma
financial information of ABN AMRO Bank N.V. at 30 September 2009 remain in ABN
AMRO Holding N.V.&#160;&#160;The remaining assets are adequately funded and
capitalised until they are transferred.&#160;&#160;The majority of these assets
will transfer during the interim period between legal demerger and legal
separation once the necessary consents have been obtained.</font></div>

at the date of legal separation, EUR 0.6 billion of these EUR 4.2 billion of
assets and EUR 0.5 billion of these EUR 4.1 billion of liabilities will remain
in ABN AMRO Holding N.V. and will be transferred as soon as possible after legal
separation.&#160;&#160;The remaining assets are adequately funded and
capitalised until their transfer after legal separation.</font></div>

liabilities that will be transferred at a later stage are presented as part of

policies.</font></font></div>

                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">Cross

        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Under article
2:334t of the Dutch Civil Code, RBS N.V., after legal demerger, remains liable
to the creditors which transferred from RBS N.V. to <font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #1b1c20">ABN AMRO Bank N.V. </font>in the event
that ABN AMRO Bank N.V. cannot meet its obligation to those
creditors.</font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The liability
relates only to obligations existing at the date of legal demerger. The
liability will cease to exist upon expiration of the obligations. RBS N.V.&#8217;s
liability is limited to the equity retained at legal demerger, amounting to
approximately EUR 4.0 billion.</font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">RBS N.V. will put
in place arrangements to mitigate the risks of the liability to the creditors
which transferred from RBS N.V. to ABN AMRO Bank N.V. by legal separation. RBS
N.V. will after legal separation hold the regulatory capital agreed with the
Dutch Central Bank for any residual risks.</font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Similarly under
Article 2:334t of the Dutch Civil Code, RBS N.V. is under certain circumstances
liable to the creditors which have transferred from RBS N.V. to New HBU II N.V.
on 7 August 2008. This liability amounts to approximately EUR 1.6 billion at 30
September 2009.</font><br></div>

        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Notes
to pro forma financial information for ABN AMRO Bank N.V. (formerly ABN AMRO II
N.V.)</font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
        <div>
          <table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%">
              <tr>
                <td valign="top" width="4%">
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">1</font></div>
                </td>
                <td valign="top" width="96%">
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">Basis
      of preparation</font></div>
                </td>
              </tr>
          </table>
        </div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The financial
information of ABN AMRO Bank N.V. as at 30 September 2009 and 31 December 2008
has been based on IFRS and IFRS as adopted by the European Union. The pro forma
financial information does not include events subsequent to 30<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#160;</font>September
2009.</font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The pro forma
financial information has been prepared on the following basis:</font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
        <div>
          <table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%">
              <tr>
                <td valign="top" width="4%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;

                </td>
                <td valign="top" width="92%">
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">The pro forma
      condensed consolidated statement of financial position of ABN AMRO Bank
      N.V. at 30 September 2009 and 31 December 2008 is presented to show the
      effect of the legal demerger of ABN AMRO Bank N.V. and is based upon the
      respective consolidated balance sheets at 30 September 2009 and 31
      December 2008 of ABN AMRO Holding N.V. as if the proposed transaction had
      occurred on 30 September 2009 and 31 December 2008.</font></div>

                <td valign="top" width="92%">
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">The pro forma
      condensed consolidated income statement of ABN AMRO Bank N.V. for the nine

                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: symbol, serif">&#183;</font></div>
                </td>
                <td valign="top" width="92%">
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">The pro forma
      condensed consolidated statement of financial position at 30 September
      2009 and 31 December 2009 for ABN AMRO Holding N.V. does not include
      residual assets left behind after the legal demerger (see note 2 for
      information on assets to be transferred after the demerger). Consequently
      the pro forma information for ABN AMRO Bank N.V. includes these residual
      assets.</font></div>
