        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
        <div>
          <table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%">
              <tr>
                <td valign="top" width="4%">
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">2</font></div>
                </td>
                <td valign="top" width="96%">
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">Assets
      and liabilities to be transferred after
demerger</font></div>
                </td>
              </tr>
          </table>
        </div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">A number of assets
and liabilities included in some Private Clients and International Diamonds
&amp; Jewellery Group businesses in branches and subsidiaries of the current ABN
AMRO Bank N.V. are not part of the demerger.&#160;&#160;These assets and
liabilities are part of the Dutch State acquired businesses and will be
transferred to ABN AMRO Bank N.V. as soon as possible after the effective date
of the demerger, when all required technical and regulatory separation
activities are completed and approvals have been obtained.</font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">At the date of
legal demerger, EUR 4.2 billion of EUR 203.0 billion of assets and EUR 4.1
billion of EUR 196.1 billion of liabilities, which are included the pro forma
financial information of ABN AMRO Bank N.V. at 30 September 2009 remain in ABN
AMRO Holding N.V.&#160;&#160;The remaining assets are adequately funded and
capitalised until they are transferred.&#160;&#160;The majority of these assets
will transfer during the interim period between legal demerger and legal
separation once the necessary consents have been obtained.</font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">It is expected that
at the date of legal separation, EUR 0.6 billion of these EUR 4.2 billion of
assets will remain in ABN AMRO Holding N.V. and will be transferred as soon as
possible after legal separation.&#160;&#160;The remaining assets are adequately
funded and capitalised until their transfer after legal separation.</font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The assets and
liabilities that will be transferred at a later stage are presented as part of
ABN AMRO Bank N.V. in the pro forma income statement and statement of financial
position as they are not significant.</font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
        <div>
          <table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%">
              <tr>
                <td valign="top" width="4%">
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">3</font></div>
                </td>
                <td valign="top" width="96%">
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">Accounting
      policies</font></div>
                </td>
              </tr>
          </table>
        </div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The same accounting
policies and methods of computation are followed in the pro forma financial
information as were applied in the preparation of the ABN AMRO Holding N.V.
financial statements for the year ended 31 December 2008, except for the impact
for the adoption of IAS 1 (revised 2007) Presentation of Financial Statements as
disclosed in the Condensed Consolidated Financial Statements for the six months
period ended 30 June 2009. <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Please refer to pages 99 to 118 of
ABN AMRO Holding N.V.&#8217;s 2008 Annual Report for a description of the accounting
policies.</font></font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>

            <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Page 15 of

              <hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
            </div>

          <div id="HDR">
            <div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right">
            </div>
          </div>
          <div>&#160;</div>
        </div>
        <div>
          <table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%">
              <tr>
                <td valign="top" width="4%">
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">4</font></div>
                </td>
                <td valign="top" width="96%">
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">Cross
      liability</font></div>
                </td>
              </tr>
          </table>
        </div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Under article
2:334t of the Dutch Civil Code ABN AMRO Bank N.V., after legal demerger, remains
liable to the creditors of RBS N.V. that remain in RBS N.V., in the event that
RBS N.V. can not meet its obligations with those creditors.</font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">The liability
relates only to obligations existing as at date of legal
demerger.&#160;&#160;The liability will cease to exist upon expiration of the
obligations.&#160;&#160;ABN AMRO Bank N.V.'s liability to creditors is limited
to the amount of equity acquired at legal demerger, which amounts to
approximately EUR 1.8 billion.</font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">ABN AMRO Bank N.V.
will put in place arrangements to mitigate the risks of the liability to the
creditors which remain with RBS N.V. by legal separation.&#160;&#160;ABN AMRO
Bank N.V. will after legal separation hold the regulatory capital agreed with
the Dutch Central Bank for any residual risks.</font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Similarly under
Article 2:334t of the Dutch Civil Code, New HBU II N.V. is under certain
circumstances liable to the creditors of RBS N.V. following the demerger from
RBS N.V. to new HBU II N.V. on 7 August 2008. This liability amounts to
approximately EUR 0.9 billion at 30 September 2009.</font><br></div>
